UCrew_rules_202.Disband crew.
- Crew members will be notified through inbox notification. 
- Disbanding a crew during crew formation allows disbanded crew members to form or join a new crew. 
- Disbanding a crew when crew formation has ended means disbanded crew members can
t take part in Crew Showdown.
Crew_rules_2Crew Showdown consist of three stages. 
In the first stage, hosts can form or join a crew. In the second stage, crew members can gain points by completing tasks. In the third stage, the top crews will receive valuable rewards according to the Crew Showdown ranking.>7
gCrew_rules_191. Change crew name, profile photo and motto.
- Changes must be reviewed and it will take some time. Once reviewed, the captain will be notified through inbox notification. 26
'QCrew_rules_18How can a captain manage the crew?
GCrew_rules_171. Hosts can form or join a crew between March 29 and April 1
2. In Form a crew, hosts can form a crew, name the crew and share invitation code or link to invite crew members.
3. In Join a crew, hosts can join a crew with an invitation code or link.
4. A host can
t be in more than one crew at the same time. A crew needs 2-10 members to take part in Crew Showdown. 
5. Crews that do not meet the qualifications will be automatically disbanded on April 1, 2022 23:59:59 (PT).+4

')Crew_rules_13Crew standards
'sCrew_rules_12Hosts who violate {CommunityGuidelines} may lose their access to the ranking and are not eligible to claim rewards.o/
ICrew_rules_11Hosts who are at least 18 years old, have access to go LIVE and residents of countries or regions where Crew Showdown is available at the moment are eligible for Crew Showdown as long as {CommunityGuidelines} are followed.
